Collected Speeches of Rev. Sun Myung Moon

Compiled by the Rev. Sun Myung Moon Speech Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the Family Federation for World Peace and Unification  Hwang Sun Jo
Rev. Sun Myung Moon, who at the age of 16 received the calling from Heaven for the salvation of humanity, has lived his entire life centered solely on the Heavenly Way! He described his life as follows:
"If Rev. Moon has any wealth, it is not from suffering for myself but from suffering for the public good; that is all the wealth I have. In social life, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. In the providential position, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. ... Until now, the teacher has received numerous oppositions and persecutions from the nation and the world. I was opposed in America, by Christianity, Judaism, and even communism. There has never been a time in history when the world has united to attack and eliminate one person like this. In that sense, the teacher is a world champion.
However, despite being cursed, I did not collapse or perish. I emerged even stronger without the slightest tremor. ... Rev. Moon insists on liberating humanity, the spirit world, hell, and even God." (Refer to Collected Speeches Vol. 105, pp. 101-103)
In one word, the life of the teacher is 'suffering itself.' The nature of this suffering is not for himself but for God and humanity. Here, we come to know who he is. The teacher is the Messiah and Savior that Christianity has hoped for over 2000 years and has come as the True Parent of humanity. Already, disciples following the teacher in 185 countries around the world are realizing the ideal of the True Family to walk the path of true children with such a confession of faith.
The teacher's self-identity is verified through his words and life. He possesses a truth that does not exist in the world. The issues of God and humans, history, and the world are clarified in his words. The promise of new words prophesied in the Bible is fulfilled within him, setting us free. These words contain 'life.' Moreover, the more important thing is that the teacher's words are merely an 'interpretation of his own life.' In other words, he himself is the truth. The Word became flesh, or incarnated. Therefore, life itself is the truth, and it comes to us through the framework of 'words.'
I am confident that readers will understand the greatness of the teacher through his words. Although the realm of the teacher's words is too high and deep to fully fathom, it fundamentally has three characteristics.
First, the teacher revealed God through his words and life. He liberated God from silence and suffering. Because humans have the bloodline of evil, they are children but cannot be called children, causing God's suffering. The teacher made the sorrowful God, who was painfully alienated due to human sin, 'speak.' He made God, who was silent and trapped in ecclesiastical authority, doctrine, and ornate buildings, 'speak,' and made God, who could not come as the parent of humanity, 'become a parent,' making the teacher the 'complete revelation of God.'
Secondly, the teacher liberated humans from ignorance and confusion. Although we humans have reasoning and can make value judgments, we cannot deny the tragic reality that we cannot fully explain our own existence. Moreover, although humans are not independent beings and are interdependent with others, they have not been able to explain that relationship. The reason is that we lost God's words. The teacher provides the ultimate answer to this. Furthermore, through a life that upholds the Heavenly Way, he shows a concrete exemplary path. Therefore, his words are living words full of life.
Thirdly, the teacher liberated the world of all things. Every object created by God has inherent value as an individual truth body. Although its value should be fully expressed under the original dominion of the original human, it was not, causing all things to groan. The teacher clarified the original value of the world of all things through his words and opened the way for the liberation of all things by restoring humans to their original state.
Rev. Moon and his wife, who have come as the eternal True Parents of humanity, continue to tirelessly give speeches around the world, demonstrating through their substantial lives the teachings of 'use the body of a servant with the heart of a parent' and 'live for the sake of others,' and work to inherit true love, true life, and true lineage.
Furthermore, through the words of life, noble life, and achievements, the teacher has finally restored and offered God's kingship as we enter the new millennium, and has settled as the king of blessed families on this earth. He has also established the Peace UN towards the Kingdom of Peace, Cheon Il Guk, the Fourth Israel, and is uniting the world into one realm of heart.
I hope that the readers who encounter these words will become the owners of Cheon Il Guk and the main actors in building the Kingdom of Peace. *

You are asked to take responsibility for education and management on behalf of Father. If there are difficulties, tell me. I can't deal with many people in the system. Come alone and report, and it will be connected to the whole, whether in America or anywhere.

You have such a long history in that channel. How many years has it been? You must synthesize everything, including coming and going to Japan. You must mediate with the government and do that. The Academic Federation and all are included in it. The Investigation Bureau and the newspaper must be managed at the top on behalf of Father and report anytime. You can't do that.

If you make the organization that way.... What kind of organization is that? The education issue instructed by Father, such as women and overall education, must have a general manager. You can't do it your way. Isn't it organized that way? "I have no greed, but...." It's more about the system. 

Song Byung-jun is now the overall head of the North Korean Five Provinces, so what was he set up for in the newspaper? He was set up in the position of representing Father. In that sense, he was entrusted with the whole. He must take overall responsibility for external activities, including the newspaper and the North Korean Five Provinces. How can you manage 10 million displaced people alone? You must make the newspaper a North Korean newspaper, centered on the displaced people. Do you understand, Kwak Chung-hwan? I told you to manage it on behalf of Father. 

Who should be entrusted with such a position? Even if there is a newspaper, the Victory Over Communism Federation, or the Academic Federation, someone must manage it on behalf of Father. In that sense, I told you to educate the whole. The person who educates must manage. That was a mistake.

"That's why Father decided it that way. We didn't do it arbitrarily. (Hwang Sun-jo)" Look, then what is Song Byung-jun? "As the publisher and president of the newspaper, he is the highest flower. So President Song Byung-jun, as the publisher and president, is the highest responsible person in the newspaper. This is objectively evaluated. (Yoo Jong-gwan)"

Look, now the vice chairman of the newspaper is in the position of moving the whole. Didn't you just say that President Song Byung-jun is below? "When Father appointed me as vice president and vice chairman in Alaska before, I mentioned that the system should be unified, not given two positions, but Father still did it that way. So now the total responsibility of the newspaper is with Vice Chairman Hwang Sun-jo. Internally and externally, President Song is under Vice Chairman Hwang, and he has decision-making power. (Kwak Chung-hwan)"

Why were you silent? "I have no position to interfere with the Segye Ilbo." Whether it's the Segye Ilbo or the system, you have a position to manage. "I wasn't in a position to interfere." Don't say that. You were entrusted with the responsibility of education and overall management on behalf of Father, weren't you? The entire world. The system was turned upside down. Do you understand? "Yes." Correct that from today.

The reason for appointing you as vice chairman was to think of Song Byung-jun as Father's representative and put him in the position of chairman. That's how you should think. The organizational system is entirely under Song Byung-jun. That's how you can use it. What can you do with a scarecrow? So his shoulders drooped, and he couldn't say anything.

"When there is a meeting of newspaper publishers at the Blue House, I can't go at all. President Song handles everything. (Hwang Sun-jo)" The system hasn't been that way until now, has it? You should be under him, not him under you. Do you understand what I'm saying? "Yes." If you are above, what does the organization become? "I don't mind how it becomes." It's not about liking it; the start was wrong. This is Kwak Chung-hwan's responsibility. I didn't think that way.

The displaced people must say that the Segye Ilbo is the newspaper of the North Korean Five Provinces
Song Byung-jun is set up to oversee the entire movement of North and South Korea on behalf of Father. The newspaper must be that way. It was centered on the women's movement, but what are you trying to do? The newspaper must move together.

So the newspaper shouldn't think of itself as a government puppet. Kwak Chung-hwan, do you understand? You must create an organization that can be directly connected to Washington. When a problem arises, you must write articles while contacting Washington immediately.

Kwak Chung-hwan! "Yes." You knew that and didn't report it to Father. Then what is Song Byung-jun? You made him a scarecrow. Even if you are a vice chairman, you are a vice chairman under Song Byung-jun, who is Father's representative. Isn't that how it should be? The organization was made that way, so it was rumored to be a Jeolla-do newspaper.

So, the spirit world cooperated. Because Korea did that at the time, it rose in the world. 'Wow, this is amazing. Korea came in fourth in the world?' they said. When the next Olympics are held, since Taekwondo is included, it will rise. With Taekwondo, 'Wow, we came in what place in Taekwondo.' It's a good time to promote Korea's name, but the problem is that there is no resolution to do so.

"In terms of providence, it seems difficult to reproduce the fourth place before unification." What unification? It's eternally difficult. "When North and South Korea are unified...." How much talent does the teacher have in various fields.... I don't want it myself. When I see it, I think, 'Why is that guy doing that?' Even when I see them training or doing something, I think that's not the way to do it. I feel that way. I've felt that way until now. 'That's a third, fifth place dropout.'

That's why when I touch it, I have to see it through to the end, so my personality is all tough. I want to see it through to the end, but if I try to see it through, I'll die quickly. What river? Longevity!

Oh, in Chuncheon.... It's Chuncheon to visit in spring and autumn. It's a place where fish that couldn't live because it was cold and left their hometown can come up.

From now on, I shouldn't curse and say this and that. The people of Chuncheon are pitiful, aren't they? Jeolla-do people or Gyeongsang-do people can be cursed a bit, but Chuncheon is pitiful, isn't it? It's a pitiful group for eternity.

Now, we have to eat and start the journey again. Do we have to leave at 9:30? "Yes." That's too early. "We can leave at 10:30." When I used to go to Chuncheon, it usually took an hour and 20 minutes. From Cheongpyeong to here is 40 minutes. It took an hour and 10 minutes round trip. During the curfew, when the siren sounded at four o'clock here, I left and returned 10 minutes before to hold a service at the headquarters here. It took 45 to 50 minutes. Now, let's eat and go. We have to go. Who's going? Are all the followers going again? "Yes." Do you need all of them? Don't you want to leave some behind? (Bows) *
